# Format probe appendix: Jet3 index TDEF + leaf-page layouts (W17a)

Generated by: `JetDatabaseWriter.FormatProbe` on 2026-04-26 21:51:39Z

This appendix grounds the W17 phase in [`index-and-relationship-format-notes.md`](index-and-relationship-format-notes.md):
**lift the "Jet3 (`.mdb` Access 97) rejects `IndexDefinition` entirely" limitation by pinning the on-disk layout of the Jet3 real-idx physical descriptor (39 bytes per mdbtools), the Jet3 logical-idx entry (20 bytes per mdbtools), and the Jet3 index leaf page (`0x04`) bitmask layout (§4.2: bitmask at `0x16`, first entry at `0xF8`).**

Each fixture below is dumped TDEF-by-TDEF for the user tables that carry at least one logical index, plus a hex dump of the first index leaf page reachable from each real-idx `first_dp`. Compare against the §3.1 / §3.2 / §4.2 mappings; mismatches indicate the spec needs amending before W17b can ship safely.

Regenerate with `dotnet run --project JetDatabaseWriter.FormatProbe`.

## `Jackcess\V1997\indexTestV1997.mdb`

- Format: Jet3Mdb, page size: 2048, code page: 1252

## `MSysAccessObjects` — TDEF page 21

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **2048**
- `num_cols` (offset 25, 2 bytes): **2**
- `num_idx` (offset 27, 4 bytes): **1**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 31, 4 bytes): **1**

| Section | Start | Size | End (excl) |
|---|---:|---:|---:|
| Page header | 0 | 8 | 8 |

| Column descriptors (numCols × 18) | 51 | 36 | 87 |
| Column names (length-prefixed) | 87 | 8 | 95 |
| Real-idx physical descriptors (numRealIdx × 39) | 95 | 39 | 134 |
| Logical-idx entries (numIdx × 20) | 134 | 20 | 154 |

| Variable trailing block (per-var-col page ptrs) | (after names) | (variable, terminated by col_num=0xFFFF) | — |

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 50 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 24 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 24 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1350
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 21
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 02 04 08 10 20 40 80 00 01 02 04 08 10 20 40 80 00 01 02 04 08).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 80 00 00 00 00 00 19 00 7F 80 00 00 01 00 00 19 06 7F 80 00 00 02 00 00 19 07 7F 80 00 00 03`

## `MSysModules2` — TDEF page 30

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **2048**
- `num_cols` (offset 25, 2 bytes): **8**
- `num_idx` (offset 27, 4 bytes): **1**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 31, 4 bytes): **1**

| Section | Start | Size | End (excl) |
|---|---:|---:|---:|

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 36 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 36 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1778
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 30
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 40 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 6F 76 7D 76 64 61 00 7F 80 00 00 02 80 7F FF FF FE 00 00 23 00 12 00 00 FF 00 0B 0C 00 06 00`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

|---|---|---:|---|

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 24 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 24 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1778
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 22
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 40 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 6F 76 7D 76 64 61 00 7F 80 00 00 02 80 7F FF FF FE 00 00 1C 00 02 00 00 13 19 7F 00 00 00 02`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 512 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 511 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 36 | yes (page_type=0x03) |

##### Resolved page 512 (`page_type = 0x03` — intermediate)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x03
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1774
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 29
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 39
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  256

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 20 00 04 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `80 7F FF F4 D3 00 00 20 62 00 00 00 25 80 7F FF FF EC 00 00 1F 00 00 00 00 26 36 ED 36 00 00 23`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 48 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 48 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 27 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 27 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1368
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 19
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 02 04 08 10 20 40 80 00 01 02 04 08 10 20 40 80 00 01 02 04 08).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 80 00 00 00 00 00 15 00 7F 80 00 00 01 00 00 15 01 7F 80 00 00 02 00 00 15 02 7F 80 00 00 03`

### Real-index physical descriptors (raw bytes per entry)

#### Real-idx #0 (offset 273, 39 bytes)

```
  0111  05 00 01 06 00 01 FF FF  00 FF FF 00 FF FF 00 FF  ................
  0121  FF 00 FF FF 00 FF FF 00  FF FF 00 FF FF 2C 02 1D  .............,..
```

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 30 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 34 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 34 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1800
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 32
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 00 00 00 00 00 00 12 08 7F 00 00 00 01 00 00 12 09 7F 00 00 00 02 00 00 12 0A 7F 00 00 00 03`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 44 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 44 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1778
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 37
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 40 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 6F 76 7D 76 64 61 00 7F 80 00 00 02 80 7F FF FF FD 00 00 2B 00 12 00 00 FF 00 0B 0C 00 06 00`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 1 | yes (page_type=0x01) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 24 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 24 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1778
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 22
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 40 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 6F 76 7D 76 64 61 00 7F 80 00 00 02 80 7F FF FF FE 00 00 1C 00 02 00 00 13 19 7F 00 00 00 02`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 2 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 2 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 32 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 38 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 38 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1800
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 34
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 00 00 00 00 00 00 13 17 7F 00 00 00 01 00 00 13 18 7F 00 00 00 02 00 00 13 19 7F 00 00 00 02`

### Real-index physical descriptors (raw bytes per entry)

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 52 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 52 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1800
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 50
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 217 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 217 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1800
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 215
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 00 00 00 00 00 00 12 08 7F 00 00 00 01 00 00 12 09 7F 00 00 00 02 00 00 12 0A 7F 00 00 00 03`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 2155 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 830 | yes (page_type=0x04) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 425 | yes (page_type=0x03) |

##### Resolved page 2155 (`page_type = 0x03` — intermediate)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x03

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 830 | yes (page_type=0x04) |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 89 | yes (page_type=0x04) |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 478 | yes (page_type=0x03) |

## `Jet3Test.mdb`

- Format: Jet3Mdb, page size: 2048, code page: 1252

## `Products` — TDEF page 20

- TDEF total bytes (after page-chain stitch): **2048**
- `num_cols` (offset 25, 2 bytes): **5**
- `num_idx` (offset 27, 4 bytes): **1**
- `num_real_idx` (offset 31, 4 bytes): **1**

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 5 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 22 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 22 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1755
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 20
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 02 04 08 10 20 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 80 00 00 01 00 00 17 00 7F 80 00 00 02 00 00 17 01 7F 80 00 00 03 00 00 17 02 7F 80 00 00 04`

### W17a leaf-page resolution probe

For each real-idx, this section probes plausible `first_dp` candidates inside the 8-byte skip entry (offset 43 + i*8) AND inside the 39-byte phys descriptor, then dumps the first page that resolves to `page_type` `0x03` (intermediate) or `0x04` (leaf).

#### Real-idx #0 candidates

| Candidate | Source bytes | Value | Resolves? |
|---|---|---:|---|
| skip entry [0..3] | LE u32 | 0 | no |
| skip entry [4..7] | LE u32 | 3 | no |
| phys desc [34..37] | LE u32 | 26 | yes (page_type=0x04) |

##### Resolved page 26 (`page_type = 0x04` — leaf)

- §4.1 header decode:
  - byte 0 page_type:    0x04
  - byte 1 unknown:      0x01
  - bytes 2..3 free_space: 1773
  - bytes 4..7 parent_page: 24
  - bytes 8..11 prev_page:  0
  - bytes 12..15 next_page: 0
  - bytes 16..19 tail_page: 0
  - bytes 20..21 pref_len:  0

- §4.2 Jet3 entry-start bitmask spans `[0x16 .. 0xF7]` inclusive (226 bytes = 1808 bits); first entry begins at `0xF8`.

- First 0x16 bytes of the bitmask (00 02 04 08 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00 00).
- First 32 bytes of the entry payload starting at 0xF8: `7F 80 00 00 01 00 00 1B 00 7F 80 00 00 02 00 00 1B 01 7F 80 00 00 03 00 00 1B 02 7F 80 00 00 04`
